    <script>
		const gambleStyle = document.querySelector(".gambling--aboveLivetable").style;
		const bocWrapper = document.getElementById("box-over-content-a");
		const breakpoint = 640;

		const mo = new MutationObserver(() => {
            if (document.querySelector(".boxOverContent--active")) {
				const bocSticky = document.querySelector(".boxOverContent--a.isSticky");
				const bocMobileSticky = document.querySelector(".boxOverContent--a.isMobileSticky");

				if (bocWrapper.getBoundingClientRect().height === 0) {
					gambleStyle.setProperty('--marginTop-noBoc', "5px");
                }

				if ((bocSticky && window.innerWidth >= breakpoint) || (bocMobileSticky && window.innerWidth < breakpoint)) {
					gambleStyle.setProperty('--top-stickyIndent', bocWrapper.getBoundingClientRect().height + "px");
					mo.disconnect();
				}
			}
        })

		const ro = new ResizeObserver(entries => {
			const bocSticky = document.querySelector(".boxOverContent--a.isSticky");
			const bocMobileSticky = document.querySelector(".boxOverContent--a.isMobileSticky");

			if (entries[entries.length -1].contentRect.height === 0) {
				gambleStyle.setProperty('--marginTop-noBoc', "5px");
			} else {
				gambleStyle.removeProperty('--marginTop-noBoc');
			}

			if ((bocSticky && window.innerWidth >= breakpoint) || (bocMobileSticky && window.innerWidth < breakpoint)) {
				gambleStyle.setProperty('--top-stickyIndent', entries[entries.length -1].contentRect.height + "px");
			} else {
				gambleStyle.removeProperty('--top-stickyIndent');
			}
		});

		const handleFranceLegalClassNames = () => {
			document.querySelectorAll(".gambling--france").forEach((element) => {
				element.classList.remove("gambling--hidden");
			});
			document.body.classList.add("legalFrance");
		}

		if (true) {
			cjs.Api.loader.get("geoIpResolver").call(function(geoIp) {
				if (geoIp === "FR") {
					handleFranceLegalClassNames();
				}
			});
        } else {
			handleFranceLegalClassNames();
		}

		mo.observe(bocWrapper, { childList: true, attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['class'], subtree: true })
		ro.observe(bocWrapper);
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function isSafari() {
        var userAgent = navigator.userAgent,
            match = userAgent.match(/(opera|chrome|crios|safari|ucbrowser|firefox|msie|trident(?=\/))\/?\s*(\d+)/i) || [],
            browser,
            tem;

        if (/trident/i.test(match[1])) {
            tem = /\brv[ :]+(\d+)/g.exec(userAgent) || [];
            return false;
        } else if (match[1] === "Chrome") {
            tem = userAgent.match(/\b(OPR|Edge)\/(\d+)/);
            if (tem && tem[1]) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        if (!browser) {
            browser = match[0].replace(/\/.*/, "");
            if (browser.indexOf("MSIE") === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            if (userAgent.match("CriOS")) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        return browser === "Safari";
    }

    const isIos = Boolean(/ipad|iphone|ipod/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent));

    if (isIos && isSafari()) {
        const img = new Image(1, 1);
        img.src = "https://flashscore.onelink.me/BvSv/2p5v0qxi";
        img.style.position = "fixed";
        document.body.appendChild(img);
    }
</script>

</footer>

<script>
	(() => {
		let legalAgeElement = document.getElementById('legal_age_confirmation');
		if(legalAgeElement){
			legalAgeElement.style.display = "none";
		}
		const cb = (globalGeoIp) => {
			const legalAgeConfirmGeoIp = ["NL"];
			if (legalAgeElement && Array.isArray(legalAgeConfirmGeoIp) && legalAgeConfirmGeoIp.includes(globalGeoIp)) {
				legalAgeElement.style.display = "block";
			}

			const recommendedSitesDisabledGeoIps = cjs.Api.config.get('app', 'disabled_pages', 'geoip') || [];
			if (recommendedSitesDisabledGeoIps.includes(globalGeoIp)) {
				document.querySelector(".selfPromo__boxItem.page-links").remove();
			}
		};
		cjs.Api.loader.get("geoIpResolver").call(cb);
	})();
</script>

            banners.addSetBackgroundCallback(function(zoneId, hasOffset){
                try {
                    var content = banners.zones[zoneId]['content'];
                    if (content.indexOf('<' + '!-- fixed -->') != -1) {
                        var envelope = document.getElementById(banners.idPrefix + zoneId);
                        if (envelope && envelope.parentElement) {
                            envelope.parentElement.style.position = 'fixed';
                        }
                    }
                } catch(pass) { }
                if (!hasOffset)
                {
                    document.body.classList.remove('background-add-off');
                    document.body.classList.add('background-add-on');
                }

                // Hide social buttons (Warning: don't remove buttongs from DOM - it is dangerous operations and breaks Firefox)
                var socialButton = document.getElementById("social-button");
                if(socialButton)
                {
                    socialButton.style.display = "none";
                }
            });


        
                    document.lsadvert_display = function() {
                        banners.display();
                                        }
                    

            if (_cjs.Api.config.get('app', 'legal_age_confirmation', 'enabled')) {
                const geoIpConf = _cjs.Api.config.get("app", "legal_age_confirmation", "geoip") || [];
                const cb = (geoIp, geoIpIsoSubdivisionCode) => {
                    if (geoIpConf.includes(geoIp)) {
                        banners.setBetting(window.localStorage.getItem("legal_age_confirmation") === "1");
                    }
                    _cjs.Api.loader.get('bannersWithBetting').fulfill((cb) => { cb(); });

                };
                _cjs.Api.loader.get('geoIpResolver').call(cb);
            }
        });

        document.displayTrustedAdvert = () => {
            cjs.Api.loader.get('cjs').call(function(_cjs) {
                _cjs.Api.loader.get('onetrust').call(() => {
                    const displayBanners = () => {
                        banners.display();
                        banners.prepareBackup(window.banners_backup_callbacks);
                    };

                    if (_cjs.Api.config.get('app', 'legal_age_confirmation', 'enabled')) {
                        _cjs.Api.loader.get('bannersWithBetting').call(() => {
                            displayBanners();
                        });
                    } else {
                        displayBanners();
                    }
                });
            });
